)@@G@@AN 'S' INSTEAD          . SINOFF    @I@@@@          SA,C3     A1,SINOFF+AY
)@@G@@3       . SAY 'ERROR' OR 'ERRORS'         . SINOFF    @I@@@@          LMAZ
)@@G@@J       X3,BTODEC         . CONVERT ERROR COUNT TO FD DEC   . SINOFF    BA
)@@G@@@I@@@@          SA,T1     A12,SINOFF+2      . STORE ERROR COUNT FOR PRINBB
)@@G@@T     . SINOFF    @I@@@@          SSL       A12,12            . GET THIRBC
)@@G@@D CHAR                  . SINOFF    @I@@@@          SA,T3     A12,SINOFFBD
)@@G@@+1      . FOR POSSIBLE LARGE ERROR COUNT  . SINOFF    @I@@@@          LABE
)@@G@@,I      A1,4              . IMAGE IS NOW 4 WORDS LONG       . SINOFF    BF
)@@G@@@I@@@@          LA        A0,FLAGCNT        . GET # OF ASM ERRORS       BG
)@@G@@      . SINOFF    @I@@@@          JZ        A0,NOER           . IF NO FLBH

)@@G@@      . SINOFF    @I@@@@          JZ        A2,PLOG3.         . IF NO ERBR
)@@G@@RORS WORTH NOTING - JUMP. SINOFF    @I@@@@          AND       A2,PFDFLGSBS
)@@G@@.       . SELECT THE FLAGS THAT ARE SET   . SINOFF    @I@@@@          LABT

)@@G@@@I@@@@          LA        A1,A3  .                                      BV
)@@G@@      . SINOFF    @I@@@@          LA        A3,BLK .                    BW
)@@G@@                        . SINOFF    @I@@@@          LDSC      A1,6   .  BX
)@@G@@                                          . SINOFF    @I@@@@          TZBY
)@@G@@        A2     .          . IS THIS FLAG SET ?              . SINOFF    BZ

)@@G@@      . SINOFF    @I@@@@.                                               CQ

)@@G@@A DEMAND USER?          . SINOFF    @I@@@@          LXI,I     A0,0100,A1CW
